architecture in Envoy v1.31.2 is built on a factory-based registration system with dynamic filter configuration support. The core mechanism consists of several key layers:\\n\\n**1. Filter Interfaces (envoy/http/filter.h)**:\\nDefines the FilterChainFactoryCallbacks interface that allows factories to register filters into the chain. Also defines StreamDecoderFilter and StreamEncoderFilter interfaces that filters must implement for request/response processing.\\n\\n**2. Filter Factory Mechanism (envoy/http/filter_factory.h)**:\\nDefines FilterFactoryCb as a function type that takes FilterChainFactoryCallbacks and instantiates filters at runtime. FilterContext carries filter metadata, FilterChainManager is the interface for applying factory callbacks, and FilterChainFactory defines the per-stream filter chain creation contract.\\n\\n**3. Filter Factory Registry (envoy/server/filter_config.h)**:\\nHttpFilterConfigFactoryBase provides the base for all HTTP filter factories. NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory and UpstreamHttpFilterConfigFactory are the two main registration interfaces for downstream and upstream filters respectively, both implementing the createFilterFactoryFromProto method.\\n\\n**4. Factory Base Classes (source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h)**:\\nCommonFactoryBase and FactoryBase provide template-based implementations that simplify filter factory creation. DualFactoryBase supports filters that work in both downstream and upstream contexts.\\n\\n**5. Filter Chain Helper and Management (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h/cc)**:\\nFilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories iterates through a list of filter factory providers and applies each factory callback to the FilterChainManager. FilterChainHelper processes proto-based filter configurations and creates factory providers with support for both static and dynamic filter config (ECDS).\\n\\n**6. Dynamic Filter Configuration (source/common/filter/config_discovery_impl.h)**:\\nNamedHttpFilterFactoryCb is a struct containing a filter name and FilterFactoryCb function. HttpDynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl manages dynamic filter discovery and instantiation, allowing filters to be loaded from xDS without restart.\\n\\n**7. Filter Manager and Execution (source/common/http/filter_manager.h/cc)**:\\nFilterManager is the core execution engine that manages the ordered list of decoder and encoder filters. It implements the FilterChainManager interface and coordinates filter execution through decodeHeaders, decodeData, decodeTrailers methods for request processing and corresponding encode methods for responses. ActiveStreamFilterBase provides per-request filter state and iteration control. FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl implements the FilterChainFactoryCallbacks to handle filter registration within the filter manager.\\n\\n**8. Connection Manager Integration (source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h/cc)**:\\nHttpConnectionManagerImpl uses FilterChainFactory to instantiate filter chains for each new HTTP stream. When a stream is created, it calls createFilterChain on the factory, which invokes applyFilterFactoryCb for each configured filter, passing the factory callbacks to register actual filter instances.\\n\\n**Extension/Chain Execution Flow**:\\nWhen a new HTTP stream arrives: (1) Connection manager calls createFilterChain on FilterChainFactory, (2) FilterChainUtility iterates filter factories and applies each to the FilterChainManager, (3) Each factory callback instantiates its filter by calling addStreamDecoderFilter/addStreamEncoderFilter on FilterChainFactoryCallbacks, (4) FilterManager maintains these filters in linked lists and executes them sequentially as data arrives, (5) Filters can stop iteration, buffer data, or inject new data, controlled by their return status codes.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3187,"cache_read_input_tokens":110468,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3187},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"0fef97d6-8d25-485c-a713-6db30eb7e256","uuid":"c760adf4-f224-4b78-a911-0348bdc7b990"}

architecture in Envoy v1.31.2 is built on a factory-based registration system with dynamic filter configuration support. The core mechanism consists of several key layers:\\n\\n**1. Filter Interfaces (envoy/http/filter.h)**:\\nDefines the FilterChainFactoryCallbacks interface that allows factories to register filters into the chain. Also defines StreamDecoderFilter and StreamEncoderFilter interfaces that filters must implement for request/response processing.\\n\\n**2. Filter Factory Mechanism (envoy/http/filter_factory.h)**:\\nDefines FilterFactoryCb as a function type that takes FilterChainFactoryCallbacks and instantiates filters at runtime. FilterContext carries filter metadata, FilterChainManager is the interface for applying factory callbacks, and FilterChainFactory defines the per-stream filter chain creation contract.\\n\\n**3. Filter Factory Registry (envoy/server/filter_config.h)**:\\nHttpFilterConfigFactoryBase provides the base for all HTTP filter factories. NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory and UpstreamHttpFilterConfigFactory are the two main registration interfaces for downstream and upstream filters respectively, both implementing the createFilterFactoryFromProto method.\\n\\n**4. Factory Base Classes (source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h)**:\\nCommonFactoryBase and FactoryBase provide template-based implementations that simplify filter factory creation. DualFactoryBase supports filters that work in both downstream and upstream contexts.\\n\\n**5. Filter Chain Helper and Management (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h/cc)**:\\nFilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories iterates through a list of filter factory providers and applies each factory callback to the FilterChainManager. FilterChainHelper processes proto-based filter configurations and creates factory providers with support for both static and dynamic filter config (ECDS).\\n\\n**6. Dynamic Filter Configuration (source/common/filter/config_discovery_impl.h)**:\\nNamedHttpFilterFactoryCb is a struct containing a filter name and FilterFactoryCb function. HttpDynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl manages dynamic filter discovery and instantiation, allowing filters to be loaded from xDS without restart.\\n\\n**7. Filter Manager and Execution (source/common/http/filter_manager.h/cc)**:\\nFilterManager is the core execution engine that manages the ordered list of decoder and encoder filters. It implements the FilterChainManager interface and coordinates filter execution through decodeHeaders, decodeData, decodeTrailers methods for request processing and corresponding encode methods for responses. ActiveStreamFilterBase provides per-request filter state and iteration control. FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl implements the FilterChainFactoryCallbacks to handle filter registration within the filter manager.\\n\\n**8. Connection Manager Integration (source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h/cc)**:\\nHttpConnectionManagerImpl uses FilterChainFactory to instantiate filter chains for each new HTTP stream. When a stream is created, it calls createFilterChain on the factory, which invokes applyFilterFactoryCb for each configured filter, passing the factory callbacks to register actual filter instances.\\n\\n**Extension/Chain Execution Flow**:\\nWhen a new HTTP stream arrives: (1) Connection manager calls createFilterChain on FilterChainFactory, (2) FilterChainUtility iterates filter factories and applies each to the FilterChainManager, (3) Each factory callback instantiates its filter by calling addStreamDecoderFilter/addStreamEncoderFilter on FilterChainFactoryCallbacks, (4) FilterManager maintains these filters in linked lists and executes them sequentially as data arrives, (5) Filters can stop iteration, buffer data, or inject new data, controlled by their return status codes.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
